    function setAttributeOnload(object, attribute, val) {
      if(window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener('load',
          function(){ object[attribute] = val; }, false);
      } else {
        window.attachEvent('onload', function(){ object[attribute] = val; });
      }
    }

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, January 13, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qbm5qFfUWvs/UtSORE3uO3I/AAAAAAAAcYc/Q__8XF9q4RY/s400/SAM_8344.JPG' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='1168877374573376182' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='1168877374573376182'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/water-meter-going-in-and-era-in.html'>Water Meter Going In, And An Era In Sacramento Ends</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1168877374573376182' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qbm5qFfUWvs/UtSORE3uO3I/AAAAAAAAcYc/Q__8XF9q4RY/s1600/SAM_8344.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qbm5qFfUWvs/UtSORE3uO3I/AAAAAAAAcYc/Q__8XF9q4RY/s400/SAM_8344.JPG" /></a>When my house guest left the house&nbsp;this morning for the airport, I could hear jackhammering down the alley.</div><br />
In a few minutes, the jackhammering was right behind my house.  I went out in my pajamas to challenge the workers.<br />
<br />
Turns out, it's a new water meter.  They've been installing these things&nbsp;all over Sacramento for years now.  I had thought they had forgotten about me.<br />
<br />
Sacramento is located at the confluence of the American and Sacramento Rivers.  There was a time in Sacramento where we could defy the rest of the state and waste water with abandon, even in the toughest of droughts.  No more.&nbsp; And era has ended.<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-N9UcAO0vVbk/UtSOQ-i9SdI/AAAAAAAAcYY/0Ocl_3jD2kA/s1600/SAM_8345.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-N9UcAO0vVbk/UtSOQ-i9SdI/AAAAAAAAcYY/0Ocl_3jD2kA/s400/SAM_8345.JPG" /></a>Concrete box and metal plate, cleverly hidden behind a plywood board so no&nbsp;Homeless Recycler&nbsp;will ever discover them.</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Wk5OhmxNLxM/UtSDq8NeYqI/AAAAAAAAcYI/iwvx389-m9o/s400/mexican-cartel-map.png' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='7389334620673392439' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='7389334620673392439'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/the-enemy-of-my-enemy-is-my-friend.html'>The Enemy Of My Enemy Is My Friend</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7389334620673392439' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Wk5OhmxNLxM/UtSDq8NeYqI/AAAAAAAAcYI/iwvx389-m9o/s1600/mexican-cartel-map.png" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Wk5OhmxNLxM/UtSDq8NeYqI/AAAAAAAAcYI/iwvx389-m9o/s400/mexican-cartel-map.png" /></a>Let's be realistic here.  The enemy of my enemy is my friend.  If the choice is between the Sinaloa Cartel and the Gulf Cartel (including psychotic Los Zetas), as it seems to be, then it's better that the U.S. work with the Sinaloa Cartel.  We don't have to like the Sinaloa folks <a href="http://www.businessinsider.com/the-us-government-and-the-sinaloa-cartel-2014-1">to do business with them</a>:<br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><blockquote>An investigation by El Universal has found that between the years 2000 and 2012, the U.S. government had an arrangement with Mexico's Sinaloa drug cartel that allowed the organization to smuggle billions of dollars of drugs in exchange for information on rival cartels.<br />
<br />
...There have long been allegations that Guzman, considered to be "the world&#8217;s most powerful drug trafficker," coordinates with American authorities.<br />
<br />
..."The DEA agents met with members of the cartel in Mexico to obtain information about their rivals and simultaneously built a network of informants who sign drug cooperation agreements, subject to results, to enable them to obtain future benefits, including cancellation of charges in the U.S.," reports El Universal, which also interviewed more than one hundred active and retired police officers as well as prisoners and experts.<br />
<br />
...El Universal said that the coordination between the U.S. and Sinaloa peaked between 2006 and 2012, which is when drug cartels consolidated their grip on Mexico. The report ends by saying that it is unclear whether the arrangements continue. <br />
</blockquote></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/more-questions-than-answers.html'>More Questions Than Answers</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2941793091240856935' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ChZvFby4XUM/UtRUHZUYQgI/AAAAAAAAcX4/nvy99YvOffE/s1600/1526671_10202867152308852_969141840_n.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ChZvFby4XUM/UtRUHZUYQgI/AAAAAAAAcX4/nvy99YvOffE/s640/1526671_10202867152308852_969141840_n.jpg" /></a></div><br />
Who are these Chosen People? What is this Promised Land? And why do we have to switch the Golden Calf for Blue Crystals?
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='750649191251791628' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='750649191251791628'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/this-bridge-scandal-is-just-starting.html'>This Bridge Scandal Is Just Starting!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-750649191251791628' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Apparently it's about money - Big Money - but the exact connections are still murky.  For reasons that are still unclear, Christie was trying to - and is still trying very hard to! - <a href="http://talkingpointsmemo.com/cafe/is-a-billion-dollar-development-project-at-the-heart-of-bridgegate">hold hostage the billion-dollar Hudson Lights project</a>:<br />
<blockquote>The Hudson Lights project is a billion dollar project because it offers unparalleled access to the George Washington Bridge. But take away that access and it&#8217;s no longer a billion dollar project.<br />
<br />
...We know that because of its location, the long-term viability of this project could be threatened by any permanent changes to the GWB toll lanes that negatively impacted the on-ramp adjacent to the site.<br />
<br />
...In other words, even though the permits were in place, the zoning approvals were done, the designs were finished, there was one last thing to lock down: the money.<br />
<br />
...Moreover, the most crucial weeks that would decide whether this project would be capitalized are coincident with the weeks between when the traffic shut-down was ordered and when the traffic shut-down was lifted. It was only after Port Authority Executive Director Patrick Foye learned of Baroni and Wildstein&#8217;s shenanigans that the financing was finally sewn up. In fact, it was the very first business day after the lanes were re-opened that the developers announced they&#8217;d raised $218 million. <br />
<br />
...I find it hard to believe that would-be investors in this project weren&#8217;t alarmed by the prospect that Port Authority officials had decided, without warning, to begin running experiments to see what would happen if local access to the GWB was temporarily, and then permanently, restricted. And in light of Mayor Sokolich&#8217;s first question to Chris Christie during their face-to-face meeting in Fort Lee this past week, asking the governor to promise not to exact revenge on Fort Lee for the trouble this scandal is causing, it seems even more significant that the governor was musing about making permanent changes in public during his December 2 press conference in Trenton. The cat was completely out of the bag on whether there had been a legitimate &#8220;traffic study,&#8221; and yet the governor persisted in characterizing the allocation of toll lanes as something that gave an unfair benefit to Fort Lee at the expense of the rest of the human race. Even in December, it seemed, Fort Lee and this project still faced a threat.<br />
<br />
...I think that begins to get at what was going on here. We now know that a major redevelopment project, one that depends on Port Authority assets and relationships, was put in jeopardy at a vulnerable financial moment, and in a way that put the viability of the entire project at risk.<br />
<br />
But we still don&#8217;t know why. </blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/breaking-bad-wins-big-at-golden-globes.html'>"Breaking Bad" Wins Big At The Golden Globes</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6677035547939861701' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<iframe width="420" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/6US3XUHZzPg" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe><br />
<br />
That was to be expected, since "Breaking Bad" is the Best TV Series Ever.<br />
<br />
This was unexpected, though:  Jennifer Lawrence apparently not wanting to intrude into Taylor Swift's interview, yet capturing the attention anyway.<br />
<br />
Similar to many people, I like Taylor Swift, but love Jennifer Lawrence.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/time-to-repair-relations-with-iran.html'>Time To Repair Relations With Iran</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-258710255438835039' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sZj-xHgmC_o/UtOng0PhXsI/AAAAAAAAcXo/SsER06eIT6c/s1600/Iran_Reboot.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sZj-xHgmC_o/UtOng0PhXsI/AAAAAAAAcXo/SsER06eIT6c/s640/Iran_Reboot.PNG" /></a>Bad relations with Iran never made much geopolitical sense.  We have too many interests in common.  It's time to reboot.</div>

<a name='238583195255865772'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/amber-if-you-could-read-my-mind.html'>Amber - If You Could Read My Mind</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-238583195255865772' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<iframe width="420" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/RaL6PXQTUD0" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe><br />
<br />
I like Amber's cover of Gordon Lightfoot's song.  She had been part of the Starz 54 trio.  Here, she is at a fashion show.<br />
<br />
<br />
<iframe width="420" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/RxR1_CTaF5o" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe><br />
<br />
These guys lip sync over her solo studio recording (from 2000, or so).  Disconcerting, but one can always choose not to look, and listen instead.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/how-breaking-bad-broke-all-of-biggie_1953.html'>How "Breaking Bad" Broke All Of Biggie Small's Crack Commandments</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7498540545352302304' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Follow these rules, you&#8217;ll have mad bread to break up<br />
If not, twenty-four years <a href="http://www.animalnewyork.com/2013/how-breaking-bad-broke-all-of-biggies-10-crack-commandments/">on the wake up</a>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/sixty-years-without-bath.html'>Sixty Years Without A Bath</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2012046149661731348' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6lzu88tuJTw/UtG86C3SlwI/AAAAAAAAcXQ/zNCOHVDCDuM/s1600/2-E4EI01m.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6lzu88tuJTw/UtG86C3SlwI/AAAAAAAAcXQ/zNCOHVDCDuM/s400/2-E4EI01m.jpg" /></a>No one knows why he <a href="http://www.viralnova.com/hasnt-bathed-60-years/">lives like this</a>.</div><br />
Impressive! Since the California rainy season has utterly failed this winter, and with water use restrictions a dead certainty, I might look like this by next November.<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-lNmot-QpBFI/UtG86E_SSvI/AAAAAAAAcXU/1iIG_2EXHUI/s1600/3-9Pf0hAX.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-lNmot-QpBFI/UtG86E_SSvI/AAAAAAAAcXU/1iIG_2EXHUI/s400/3-9Pf0hAX.jpg" /></a>Likes to smoke a pipe filled with animal dung.<br />
<br />
Damn, this guy is a role model!</div><br />
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZkZoC_7Kv8Y/UtG6BZpcJLI/AAAAAAAAcW8/DkgIvLPmkkc/s400/1526953_453459508114070_1394049856_n.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5645577390621418119' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5645577390621418119'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/i-want-to-believe.html'>I Want To Believe</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5645577390621418119' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZkZoC_7Kv8Y/UtG6BZpcJLI/AAAAAAAAcW8/DkgIvLPmkkc/s1600/1526953_453459508114070_1394049856_n.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZkZoC_7Kv8Y/UtG6BZpcJLI/AAAAAAAAcW8/DkgIvLPmkkc/s400/1526953_453459508114070_1394049856_n.jpg" /></a>From <a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/BreakingRomania/">Breaking Bad Friends</a>.</div><br />
From a 2011 review in Salon by Matt Zoller Seitz: <br />
<blockquote>"Breaking Bad" is, in its heart, the story of the supposedly respectable, white, upper-middle class becoming the Other. I don't think it's an accident that those quasi-mythic drawings of Walt in the guise of his porkpie-hatted alter ego, Heisenberg, resemble old Project Bluebook sketches of extraterrestrial visitors. Walt is becoming as much an alien -- an undesirable Other -- as the illegals who have periodically sneaked across the border throughout the show's run.</blockquote><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_wY0EkGZjHg/UtG6Bfb-PfI/AAAAAAAAcXA/75F-w9aLseQ/s1600/1484292_453460698113951_870321040_n.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_wY0EkGZjHg/UtG6Bfb-PfI/AAAAAAAAcXA/75F-w9aLseQ/s400/1484292_453460698113951_870321040_n.jpg" /></a>Which reminds me of the only time I ever <a href="http://www.nuforc.org/webreports/096/S96946.html">reported a UFO sighting</a>.</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WzzmDOPVziw/UtG1CodytcI/AAAAAAAAcWs/OFochrAMFkQ/s400/4d34a765ac429_image.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/jeff-brofsky-will-be-at-albuquerque.html'>Jeff Brofsky Will Be At Albuquerque Comic Con</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4203037238136071917' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WzzmDOPVziw/UtG1CodytcI/AAAAAAAAcWs/OFochrAMFkQ/s1600/4d34a765ac429_image.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WzzmDOPVziw/UtG1CodytcI/AAAAAAAAcWs/OFochrAMFkQ/s400/4d34a765ac429_image.jpg" /></a>It's time for Albuquerque Comic Con, and that means it's time for Jeff Brofsky!  Here is brand-new profile of Jeff:</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><br />
</div><blockquote>Brofsky's love for comic books goes back to his days as a youngster, growing up in Far Rockaway, N.Y. He still remembers his father, a lieutenant with the NYPD, giving him a buck and telling him to select 10 comic books.<br />
<br />
Although his dad seemed to prefer that he pick out favorites like Superman and Batman, the youngster "wanted Marvel (brand) X-Men, Spider Man ("the first hero of the Silver Age of comics," Brofsky says), Fantastic Four." He wouldn't let his father read his new comics because he didn't like the way his dad bent the covers back when he read them, almost as if Jeff Brofsky anticipated a price guide coming out sometime in the future, with incredibly high prices for those in "mint" condition.<br />
<br />
Some of those old titles are still some of his favorites.<br />
<br />
"I still have a lot of stuff," he said. He keeps his best comics, including some top-dollar items, in a safe deposit box, and keeps his prized comics in mint condition by not reading them. Many of his old favorites have been reprinted in volumes of hardback books.<br />
<br />
...Brofsky's parents moved the family, apparently part of that great Empire State migration, to Rio Rancho in 1972, right after Brofsky graduated high school. Brofsky said some Rio Ranchoans may remember his name in the Observer several decades ago, when he donned a costume to be "Chicken Man" at New Mexico Six Guns' hockey games at Tingley Coliseum.<br />
<br />
He attended the University of New Mexico, where he ultimately obtained his bachelor's degree in psychology.<br />
<br />
"I use it every day," he says of that degree, although a marketing degree might have suited him better for his Tall Tales Comics venture. Although his passion had once been stamps and coins - he remembered organizing his own show for those hobbies in New York - comic books remained a passion when he was an adult.</blockquote>I went on two Vegas weekends.  Since what happens in Vegas ends up on my blog, here is <a href="http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2006/01/clubbin-in-las-vegas-besides-myself.html">that report</a>.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Friday, January 10, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='8350144823205306013' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='8350144823205306013'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/i-have-house-guest.html'>I Have A House Guest!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8350144823205306013' itemprop='description articleBody'>
I've been in my house for nearly nineteen years.  I've never had a house guest before!  Shake things up a bit!<br />
<br />
He went on a walk this morning.  Who does that?<br />
<br />
Curious if E. has met him by now:<br />
<br />
M.:  Say hello when he returns from his walk.<br />
<br />
E.:  I'll hide in my bedroom when <i>mokum</i> comes back.  <br />
<br />
M.:  No, be sure to say hello!  He's a nice guy!
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/so-chris-christies-got-himself-scandal.html'>So, Chris Christie's Got Himself A Scandal</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6275639121059975410' itemprop='description articleBody'>
It figures a bully like him would <a href="http://talkingpointsmemo.com/livewire/christie-statement-bridge">do something like this</a>:<br />
<blockquote>&#8220;What I've seen today for the first time is unacceptable," Christie said. "I am outraged and deeply saddened to learn that not only was I misled by a member of my staff, but this completely inappropriate and unsanctioned conduct was made without my knowledge."</blockquote>I like a <a href="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2014/01/08/1268171/-Christie-s-bridge-outrage-doesn-t-stop-the-questions-or-the-jokes">tweet</a> posted at Daily Kos:<br />
<blockquote>If you think Gov. Christie wasn't involved in closing the lanes to the bridge, then I have a bridge to sell you.<br />
&#8212; @zachbraff </blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, January 07, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2906386876168048738' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2906386876168048738'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/rush-limbaugh-meteorologist.html'>Rush Limbaugh, Meteorologist</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2906386876168048738' itemprop='description articleBody'>
He's an ass, but he <a href="http://www.salon.com/2014/01/07/rush_limbaugh_polar_vortex_is_a_hoax_created_by_the_left/">makes me laugh</a>, sometimes.<br />
<br />
The trouble is that Meteorologist speak is slowly bleeding into common English usage.  Weather guys talk like this all the time.  At least the 'polar vortex' crisis of 2014 isn't as severe as the 'haboob' crisis of 2011 and 2012, when Arizona was hit unusually hard by these dust storms, and people all over the state freaked out about lurid-edged Arabic words contaminating the pristine way they speak out in the 602:<blockquote>We are having a record-breaking cold snap in many parts of the country. And right on schedule the media have to come up with a way to make it sound like it&#8217;s completely unprecedented. Because they&#8217;ve got to find a way to attach this to the global warming agenda, and they have. It&#8217;s called the &#8220;polar vortex.&#8221; The dreaded polar vortex.<br />
<br />
Do you know what the polar vortex is? Have you ever heard of it? Well, they just created it for this week&#8230;They&#8217;re in the middle of a hoax, they&#8217;re perpetrating a hoax, but they&#8217;re relying on their total dominance of the media to lie to you each and every day about climate change and global warming.<br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/made-buzzworthy.html'>Made Buzzworthy!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2750365512735860891' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Dave Layman noticed <a href="http://www.buzzfeed.com/lukelewis/this-might-be-the-sweetest-walter-white-tribute-yet">this Buzzworthy article</a> that appeared last October regarding the descanso my sister and myself made.  Somehow, I missed it, but it's cute:<br />
<blockquote>"This Might Be The Sweetest Walter White Tribute Yet"</blockquote>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/clickworthy.html'>Clickworthy</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2725728830177842296' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://finance.yahoo.com/news/selling-social-media-clicks-becomes-151602216.html">Not</a>:<br />
<blockquote>For as little as a half cent each click, websites hawk everything from LinkedIn connections to make members appear more employable to Soundcloud plays to influence record label interest. <br />
<br />
...Italian security researchers and bloggers Andrea Stroppa and Carla De Micheli estimated in 2013 that sales of fake Twitter followers have the potential to bring in $40 million to $360 million to date, and that fake Facebook activities bring in $200 million a year. <br />
<br />
...Dhaka, Bangladesh, a city of 7 million in South Asia, is an international hub for click farms. <br />
<br />
The CEO of Dhaka-based social media promotion firm Unique IT World said he has paid workers to manually click on clients' social media pages, making it harder for Facebook, Google and others to catch them. "Those accounts are not fake, they were genuine," Shaiful Islam said. <br />
<br />
...In 2013, the State Department, which has more than 400,000 likes and was recently most popular in Cairo, said it would stop buying Facebook fans after its inspector general criticized the agency for spending $630,000 to boost the numbers. <br />
<br />
...In Indonesia, a social media-obsessed country with some of the largest number of Facebook pages and Twitter users, click farms proliferate. <br />
<br />
Ali Hanafiah, 40, offers 1,000 Twitter followers for $10 and 1 million for $600. He owns his own server, and pays $1 per month per Internet Protocol address, which he uses to generate thousands of social media accounts. <br />
<br />
...David Burch, at TubeMogul, a video marketing firm based in Emeryville, Calif., said that buying clicks to promote clients is a grave error. "It's bad business," he said, "and if an advertiser ever found out you did that, they'd never do business with you again." <br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/charity-as-form-of-kickback.html'>Charity As A Form Of Kickback</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5078805715844392176' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Pharmaceutical prices are <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2013/12/19/business/shake-up-at-big-co-pay-fund-raises-scrutiny-on-similar-charities.html?_r=0">way too high</a>:<br />
<blockquote>As drug prices have soared in recent years and insurers have increased co-payments, a new type of charity has blossomed to fill a vital niche &#8212; helping patients pay the steep out-of-pocket costs for their medicines. <br />
 <br />
But the largest of these co-payment assistance charities, the Chronic Disease Fund, is now in turmoil after questions have arisen about its relationship with a pharmaceutical company that is itself under investigation for its marketing practices. <br />
<br />
The practice is casting light on what has long been an open secret: The bulk of the contributions to these charities come from the pharmaceutical companies. The foundations not only help hundreds of thousands of patients a year, they also raise drug company sales and profits. <br />
<br />
After all, if a patient cannot afford out-of-pocket costs of $5,000 for a $100,000-a-year drug, the drug company gets nothing. But if the manufacturer or the charity pays the $5,000, the patient gets the drug and the company receives $95,000 from the patient&#8217;s insurance company or Medicare. <br />
<br />
...Critics say co-pay assistance helps keep drug prices high and circumvents efforts by insurers to control drug spending by making consumers bear part of the cost. <br />
<br />
&#8220;These subsidies are unfortunately used to promote the overutilization of expensive brand-name drugs,&#8221; said Wells Wilkinson, a lawyer at Community Catalyst, a consumer advocacy organization. <br />
<br />
The charities counter that any benefit to the drug companies is secondary to helping patients. <br />
<br />
&#8220;Look at the alternative,&#8221; said Dana Kuhn, founder and president of Patient Services, one of the charities. &#8220;If they didn&#8217;t donate their dollars, people would die.&#8221; <br />
<br />
Drug companies often directly subsidize the co-payments for privately insured patients. But they cannot do so for patients covered by federal programs like Medicare&#8217;s Part D drug benefit, because that would be considered a kickback, an illegal inducement to use a drug. <br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, January 06, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='7555524051867263150' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='7555524051867263150'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/wonder-how-pamela-trokanskis-plans-will.html'>Wonder How Pamela Trokanski's Plans Will Affect DMTC?</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7555524051867263150' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://www.davisenterprise.com/local-news/local-woman-looks-to-introduce-life-in-11-dimensions/">Synergy?  Competition?  Trouble?  Success?</a>:<br />
<blockquote>Trokanski is fixing to build an 18,000-square-foot, two-story building next to her current studio that will introduce what she calls &#8220;Life in 11 Dimensions,&#8221; which will bring together a spa, healthy meals, dancing, art, theatrical productions and a community meeting space.<br />
<br />
...According to a professionally drawn site plan for the project, a full 3,438 square feet can be devoted to meeting places for community groups, business conferences and the community, with a dedicated nearby space for the healthy food vendor Stone Soup to provide on-site catering. Produce could come from an on-site organic garden. A theater will have 115 to 200 seats depending on the production.<br />
<br />
&#8220;It&#8217;s kind of a gift to Davis,&#8221; Trokanski said. &#8220;Living a healthy, creative life in a healthy, creative community in a healthy, creative world.&#8221;<br />
<br />
Collaboration is the name of the game. Acme Theatre Company, a longtime troupe for high school-aged actors, is just one of several groups looking to benefit from &#8220;11D,&#8221; as the project is being called.<br />
<br />
&#8220;We&#8217;ve been thinking of a collaborative space, so when Pamela talked about 11D it seemed just like a dream,&#8221; said Emily Henderson, artistic director of Acme. Henderson first met Trokanski as her student at a dance class at Davis High School, an example of the roots Trokanski has in the community.<br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/oak-park-heads-balletward.html'>Oak Park Heads Balletward</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6642614803827476223' itemprop='description articleBody'>
They are onto <a href="http://www.sacbee.com/2013/12/21/6019951/girls-self-esteem-program-academy.html">something good</a>:<blockquote>Denver Russell has the chance of a lifetime. She will star in what&#8217;s believed to be Oak Park&#8217;s first rendition of the classic ballet &#8220;The Nutcracker.&#8221;<br />
<br />
&#8220;It means a lot to me,&#8221; the bashful 10-year-old said last week.<br />
<br />
Denver is one of 40 girls in the Girls Self-Esteem Program Academy who are practicing their dance moves around the clock and honing their pointe technique by balancing on their toes. <br />
<br />
...Girls in the program, ages 4 to 18, practice ballet three times a week and pay between $25 and $50 a month to participate. Most of the girls are black and hail from underprivileged families from across the Sacramento region, said Kandice Kelly, the program&#8217;s director.<br />
<br />
&#8220;I&#8217;m of the belief that every girl in the world should take ballet once,&#8221; said Kelly, a former ballerina. &#8220;It helps with poise. It helps with grace.&#8221;<br />
<br />
Kelly founded the program five years ago after volunteering at the Fathers Resource Center, a nonprofit for single fathers that she discovered while working as a television news reporter.<br />
<br />
&#8220;There were a lot of girls who didn&#8217;t have mothers. And the little girls started following me on the weekends because I was the only female,&#8221; Kelly said.<br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/obnoxious-bureaucrats.html'>Obnoxious Bureaucrats</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5001432281015659586' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Al Qaeda is apparently <a href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/060-cake-al-qaida-records-every-expense">very meticulous</a>:<br />
<blockquote>This transaction in northern Mali shows what might seem an unusual preoccupation for a terror group: Al-Qaida is obsessed with documenting the most minute expenses.<br />
<br />
In more than 100 receipts left in a building occupied by al-Qaida in the Islamic Maghreb in Timbuktu earlier this year, the extremists assiduously tracked their cash flow, recording purchases as small as a single light bulb. The often tiny amounts are carefully written out in pencil and colored pen on scraps of paper and Post-it notes: The equivalent of $1.80 for a bar of soap; $8 for a packet of macaroni; $14 for a tube of super glue. All the documents were authenticated by experts.</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/nice-article-on-liorah-singerman.html'>Nice Article On Liorah Singerman</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6545521078319410206' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://www.insidepublications.org/index.php/local-heroes/592-way-off-broadway">Theater busy</a>:<blockquote>&#8220;My mother was a teacher in the Sacramento school district,&#8221; says Singerman, &#8220;so I knew how much performing arts were suffering in the schools. It was just horrible.&#8221; That first season, she spent 90 minutes a week for 10 weeks with students at Caroline Wenzel Elementary School in Greenhaven. They produced a review that was a huge success.<br />
<br />
Five years later, Singerman is juggling shows at five schools&#8212;Didion, Crocker Riverside, Sutterville, Holy Spirit, and Shalom School&#8212;as well as a production of &#8220;The Wizard of Oz&#8221; at Sierra 2 Center for the Arts and Community in Curtis Park. That production will be taken to the participating schools, which simplifies the logistics of sets, lighting, costumes and choreography. Singerman&#8212;relying on her husband&#8217;s skills&#8212;has introduced the use of film to project the stage sets. &#8220;We rearranged our living room and set up a green screen, just like they use for weather reports,&#8221; says Plaza. &#8220;The kids came over and we shot footage.&#8221;<br />
<br />
Singerman choreographs, directs and produces every show, with help from husband and assistant director Michelle Petro. Parents do everything from selling tickets and refreshments at the shows to ensuring that Young Actors Stage has a home at their children&#8217;s schools.<br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/say-what-you-think.html'>Say What You Think</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6399900214507879612' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<a href="http://talkingpointsmemo.com/livewire/iraq-fallujah-white-house-obama-republicans-mccain-graham">Good point</a>:<br />
<blockquote>Following reports that the Iraqi city of Fallujah had fallen into the control of an al Qaida-affiliated group over the weekend, Sens. John McCain (R-AZ) and Lindsey Graham (R-SC) wasted little time in putting out a statement blaming the tumult on the Obama administration's decision to withdraw U.S. forces from the country in 2011.<br />
<br />
...White House press secretary Jay Carney said Monday that the likes of McCain and Graham ought to be transparent about what exactly they're proposing.<br />
<br />
"I've heard members of Congress suggest this, but if members were suggesting that there should be American troops fighting and dying in Fallujah today, they should say so," Carney said during his daily press briefing.<br />
</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<a name='6454125750988182197'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/thrown-under-bus.html'>Thrown Under The Bus</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6454125750988182197' itemprop='description articleBody'>
In the end, everyone abandoned Liz Cheney.  And it's a <a href="http://www.salon.com/2014/01/06/tea_party_debacle_implodes_liz_cheney_quits_senate_race/">good thing!</a>:<br />
<blockquote>Cheney&#8217;s early 2014 struggles had a lot to do with the flaws of her own campaign, and now she says family concerns ultimately doomed her bid. But I think her already-flailing debacle of a campaign (before the family news came out) tells us something about the fizzling of the Tea Party as an oppositional force, especially when it comes to serious, entrenched conservatives like Wyoming&#8217;s Mike Enzi. It bodes well for 2014 that she flamed out quickly. Nepotistic sister-betraying Cheneys and other Tea Party opportunists just may not find Republican primaries as easy as they were in 2010. And that&#8217;s good for both parties, and for the country.</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/a-happy-ending.html'>A Happy Ending!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4902318563681801482' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Amanda sends a happy note:<blockquote>UPDATE: Alex is found! Thank you! Thank you to all who helped. He had located a river and was found following it. Stayed in the woods 2 nights. He is tired, hungry, and disoriented but otherwise well. Sooo many people came out for the search. Wouldn't have found him without you and the shares</blockquote>

          <div class="date-posts">

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/search-starting-for-alex-salyers.html'>Search Starting For Alex Salyers</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6545419095580898834' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Search starting early tomorrow morning for Amanda's brother, in the Sierra foothills vicinity of Cool, CA.  <blockquote>My dear mountain friends: My brother Alex has been missing since last night. He may have just wandered off, but no one knows where he is and we'd like to know he is safe. Last seen walking towards Auburn Lake Trails. Please let me know if you have any info.</blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

I am puzzled. Where is the moral? But it's five minutes till curtain, so must run....

<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='8338292656349568615' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='8338292656349568615'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/first-weekend-of-cabaret-done.html'>First Weekend Of "Cabaret" Done</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8338292656349568615' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Was this just the most-endless Tech Week, or what?  A performance or rehearsal on ten of the last eleven days!  Endurance was useful for Stage Managing this show, but with a lingering cold, it was hard to find, at times.  I'd fall into coughing jags, and had other issues.<br />
<br />
New Year's Eve went pretty well.  The cast was motivated!<br />
<br />
Friday night, there were some glitches - people missing set changes, usually.  Twice, I snagged the line leading from my head set to the radio transmitter while moving furniture, which disconnected me from the headset and delayed relaying 'Lights!' to Jenna in the Light Booth.<br />
<br />
Saturday night was nearly-perfect for set changes.  Just some prop problems (Letter to England, etc.).  Dalton told a few tales - about how he and Katherine inadvertently spat into each other's faces, and the like.  There was a distraction too.  Katherine came onstage in her fur coat towards the end of Act I.  She took off the fur coat and laid it down.  Just then, a highly-visible moth came out of the fur coat, and started buzzing about on stage.  Strange!<br />
<br />
Sunday afternoon, a few set change issues returned.  At the end of the first Train scene, Hugo exited stage right again, instead of stage left.  With him delayed, that set change turned into a massive clusterfrack stage left.  Richard and I nearly collided while changing the set just before 'Sitting Pretty', which definitely slowed things down.  Katherine noticed the last egg remaining for the weekend was very-strangely puckered and distorted.  We wanted to make Dalton eat it on stage, or at least see if there was a bat inside of it, or something, but thought better of it, and sent Rebecca out to get more eggs instead.<br />
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>
<div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'><span class='post-author vcard'>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/john-wesley-powell-suggested-these.html'>John Wesley Powell Suggested These State Boundaries In The West</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6434273074625676863' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jJ-_nSjkBBU/UsdGcIDgzwI/AAAAAAAAcWA/FypsWsvulLY/s1600/Powell_Map.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jJ-_nSjkBBU/UsdGcIDgzwI/AAAAAAAAcWA/FypsWsvulLY/s640/Powell_Map.jpg" /></a><br />
The idea was to <a href="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2014/01/02/1257121/-The-United-Watershed-States-of-America">mitigate struggles over water</a>.  Didn't happen, though.</div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/blakes-is-opening-their-first.html'>Blake's Is Opening Their First Restaurant Outside New Mexico</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7684584765015132404' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Sixty-one years! <a href="http://www.abqjournal.com/327350/news/blakes-to-open-first-restaurant-outside-nm.html">'bout time!</a>:<blockquote>The popular Albuquerque-based hamburger chain will open its new El Paso restaurant the first week of January, according to a company executive.<br />
<br />
It will be the only Blake&#8217;s Lotaburger located outside of New Mexico &#8212; at least for now. A second El Paso location is planned for the spring.</blockquote><br />
I've been surprised Blake's hasn't expanded beyond the state boundaries, till now.  El Paso is a natural target for an expanding operation. Besides, according to K., El Paso restaurant choices suck, so anything that can be done to help.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KNf6NvwzFcQ/Usc6HqfZc_I/AAAAAAAAcVw/WuWCa_WA1Zo/s640/24_cmmdr-r-jordan.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='2088115735709106931' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='2088115735709106931'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/2014-year-of-troubles.html'>2014 - Year Of Troubles</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2088115735709106931' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KNf6NvwzFcQ/Usc6HqfZc_I/AAAAAAAAcVw/WuWCa_WA1Zo/s1600/24_cmmdr-r-jordan.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KNf6NvwzFcQ/Usc6HqfZc_I/AAAAAAAAcVw/WuWCa_WA1Zo/s640/24_cmmdr-r-jordan.jpg" /></a>Lt. Commander Rebecca Jordan, hero of Smog Town troops in the Battle of Interstate 5.</div><br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
Well, the forecasts are <a href="https://www.fnmoc.navy.mil/wxmap_cgi/cgi-bin/wxmap_loop.cgi?&amp;area=nvg_namer&amp;prod=prp&amp;dtg=2014010318&amp;set=All">beginning to weaken</a> the small potential storm next Thursday to nothingness, and strengthening the eastern Pacific ridge again. 2014 is going to be a year of locusts in California. And that's really bad, because my entire life-plan is based on the Grasshopper, not the Ant.  Time to revisit <a href="http://www.sandowbirk.com/paintings/the-great-war-of-the-californias/">"The Great War of the Californias"</a>. <br />
<br />
Among the holdings at the <a href="http://www.dirosaart.org/">Di Rosa Art Museum</a> near Napa, they actually have the immense canvas of "The Battle of San Francisco". Amazing panorama! <br />
<br />
Here's a <a href="http://www.zimbio.com/watch/YWw5s77C_Lc/Smog+Thunder+Great+War+Californias/In+Smog+And+Thunder+The+Great+War+Of+The+Californias">trailer</a>.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>

<a name='1495734318677488672'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/ice-box.html'>Ice Box</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1495734318677488672' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Kathleen in Calgary <a href="http://www.theatlantic.com/technology/archive/2014/01/right-now-its-as-cold-in-canada-as-where-our-rover-is-on-mars/282775/">notes this</a>:<blockquote>This week, in Southern Manitoba, the temperature reached a blisteringly frigid -31 degrees Celsius, or nearly -24 Fahrenheit. (Wind chill values in Winnipeg&#8212;in case you were curious and/or in need of some meteorological schadenfreude&#8212;dipped to -58 Fahrenheit.) Which is crazy, and which makes for, as <a href="http://ca.news.yahoo.com/blogs/geekquinox/frigid-winnipeg-temperatures-reach-cold-planet-mars-204225571.html">Yahoo's Geekquinox blog</a> puts it, "the coldest afternoon temperatures the area has seen in several years." <br />
<br />
...And over the past month, Yahoo notes, REMS has been reporting daily high temperatures on Mars that range from -25 to -31 degrees Celsius. (Mars seems to be having its own cold spell: The -31 degrees Celsius temperature is the coldest daily high the rover has recorded since it landed on the planet in August 2012.) </blockquote>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, January 02, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6506121711861587840' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6506121711861587840'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/internal-siamese-twin.html'>Internal Siamese Twin</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6506121711861587840' itemprop='description articleBody'>
(Standing in the sandwich line at Subway.  IST observes me looking at my iPhone while holding it just inches in front of my left eye)<br />
<br />
IST: You shouldn't hold the iPhone so close to your eye.  It will damage your retina.  Like a TV.  Instead, you should use a magnifying glass while holding the iPhone at arm's length.<br />
<br />
M.:  I had retinal surgery in 1994.  They put a band around my eye, so it's even more near-sighted than it used to be.<br />
<br />
IST:  You should have a doctor look at that.  It's better to be safe than sorry.  Not that I want to intrude.  You should have a doctor look at that.  It's better to be safe than sorry.  Not that I want to intrude. You should have a doctor look at that.  It's better to be safe than sorry.  Not that I want to intrude......<br />
<br />
M.:  (Observing his three foot-long sandwiches being made) That's a lot of food.  It's not just for yourself, is it?<br />
<br />
IST:  Yes, it is.  I have two stomachs.  In the womb, I started to divide into a Siamese twin, but the process didn't complete.  I'm an Internal Siamese Twin.<br />
<br />
M.:  So, do you have a split personality?<br />
<br />
IST:  No, although I have mood swings.  The process didn't complete.  I should have a doctor look at that.<br />
<br />
M.:  So, you're going to eat all those sandwiches?<br />
<br />
IST:  Yes.  It's really something when the stomach on the left starts growling, and the stomach on the right starts growling too.  I need the nutrition.  It's part of being an Internal Siamese Twin.  The process didn't complete, so I have just one heart, just behind the breast bone, almost in the center of the chest.<br />
<br />
M.:  My breast bone is messed up, maybe from a lack of nutrition when I was three years old.<br />
<br />
IST:  You should have a doctor look at that.  It's better to be safe than sorry.  Particularly the Vitamin C.  You can get the scurvies from that.<br />
<br />
M.:  They used to get that on sailing ships.<br />
<br />
IST:  They'd lose two thirds of the crew to the scurvies.  Your hair falls out and you get yellow eye balls.  Your membranes basically fall apart.  It's so important what women eat when they are pregnant, especially in the first three weeks.  That's when the cell division occurs, and when Siamese twins get made. (To the 'sandwich artist') Can you add more pickles?<br />
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/small-storm-over-horizon.html'>Small Storm Over The Horizon</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2542191011337120686' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Extended weather forecasts are beginning to show a <a href="https://www.fnmoc.navy.mil/wxmap_cgi/cgi-bin/wxmap_loop.cgi?&area=nvg_epac&prod=prp&dtg=2014010218&set=All">possible small storm</a> in northern California in about a week - next Thursday. I certainly hope so. The drought situation has never been so desperate in California! 2014 is setting up as a real ugly year for water, and we need as much as possible, as often as possible, and right the hell now.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='3862660' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='3044009102188073283' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='3044009102188073283'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/mr-doesnt-like-confrontation-confronts.html'>Mr. Doesn't-Like-Confrontation Confronts</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3044009102188073283' itemprop='description articleBody'>
Mr. Doesn't-Like-Confrontation confronted homeless bicyclist with dog leaning against my garage door at 5 a.m. "I had to poop. I'll clean it up." Um, OK.<br />
<br />
Spied on him a few times.  What is with this dude? Now he's counting out money.<br />
<br />
Fellow lingered under the driveway light for about an hour. I finally called Sac PD, but just then he pushed on. Not eager to check on situation downstairs. Fellow was at least apologetic: no Marcy-Darcy crap.<br />
<br />
In the morning, went down to check.  Looks like homeless guy tried to break into the garage, and smeared shit on the outside wall. Charming!<br />
<br />
Can't find his shit.  I wonder where he put it?  Doesn't seem to be in the garbage cans.<br />
<br />
So, who is this guy?  A new nutter in the 'hood....
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2014/01/sorry-for-lack-of-posting.html'>Sorry For Lack Of Posting</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2441707793772272086' itemprop='description articleBody'>
With crazy work schedule, opening of 'Cabaret', holiday visits, and feeling sick, I just haven't had the time.  Fell behind too.  The world is moving on at light speed....
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2013/12/nearly-got-side-swiped-on-freeway-last.html'>Nearly Got Side-Swiped On The Freeway Last Night</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-9167321062576520575' itemprop='description articleBody'>
I was slowly passing a car on the left, and was momentarily in the driver's blind spot, just when the driver decided to make a lane change.  We <i>almost</i> collided.<br />
<br />
Scary!
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://marcvaldez.blogspot.com/2013/12/northern-new-mexican-accent.html'>Northern New Mexican Accent </a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7277251913744341343' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<iframe width="420" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/ehUJTIgn_Dk" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe><br />
<br />
Students from Las Vegas give examples of the accent.  The funniest part is the accented disembodied voice who takes the fast food order.
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
